### Fuel Cell `http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/FuelCell`
#### Removed
- [Fuel Cell](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/FuelCell) [definition](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/definition) "An Electrical Power Source that consists in part of an anode, a cathode, and an electrolyte; converts chemical energy from a fuel into electricity through a chemical reaction of positively charged hydrogen ions with an oxidizing agent (typically oxygen); and, if given a continuous source of fuel and oxidizing agent, can continuously produce electricity."@en 

- [Fuel Cell](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/FuelCell) [elucidation](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/elucidation) "A Fuel Cell differs from a Battery in that it requires a continuous source of fuel and oxygen to sustain the chemical reaction, whereas a Battery only uses chemicals already stored inside it."@en 

#### Added
- [Fuel Cell](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/FuelCell) [scopeNote](http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#scopeNote) "A Fuel Cell differs from a Battery in that it requires a continuous source of fuel and oxygen to sustain the chemical reaction, whereas a Battery only uses chemicals already stored inside it."@en 

- [Fuel Cell](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/FuelCell) [definition](http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#definition) "An Electrical Power Source that consists in part of an anode, a cathode, and an electrolyte; converts chemical energy from a fuel into electricity through a chemical reaction of positively charged hydrogen ions with an oxidizing agent (typically oxygen); and, if given a continuous source of fuel and oxidizing agent, can continuously produce electricity."@en

IFVs also often have improved armour and firing ports (allowing the infantry to fire personal weapons while mounted)."@en

### Payload `http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/Payload`
#### Removed
- [Payload](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/Payload) [definition](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/definition) "A Material Entity that is transported by a Vehicle during an Act of Location Change for the purpose of being delivered to or performing one or more functions at a predefined location."@en 

- [Payload](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/Payload) [elucidation](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/elucidation) "In each case, the Payload is what provides the immediate reason for performing the Act of Location Change (e.g. transporting the passengers of a commercial airline flight to their destination; transporting food, fuel, oxygen, research equipment, and spare parts to the International Space Station; or conveying an array of sensors, cameras, and communications systems so they can operate during a Sun-Synchronous Earth Orbit)."@en 

#### Added
- [Payload](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/Payload) [definition](http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#definition) "A Material Entity that is transported by a Vehicle during an Act of Location Change for the purpose of being delivered to or performing one or more functions at a predefined location."@en 

- [Payload](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/Payload) [scopeNote](http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#scopeNote) "In each case, the Payload is what provides the immediate reason for performing the Act of Location Change (e.g. transporting the passengers of a commercial airline flight to their destination; transporting food, fuel, oxygen, research equipment, and spare parts to the International Space Station; or conveying an array of sensors, cameras, and communications systems so they can operate during a Sun-Synchronous Earth Orbit)."@en

- [Propelling Nozzle](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/PropellingNozzle) [definition](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/definition) "A Nozzle that is used to convert a propulsion Engine into a Jet Engine and functions by using its narrowest part, the throat, to increase Pressure within the Engine by constricting flow, usually until the flow chokes, then expanding the exhaust stream to, or near to, atmospheric pressure, while forming it into a high speed jet to propel the Vehicle."@en

- [Resource](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/Resource) [definition](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/definition) "A Continuant that is owned by, in the possession of, or is otherwise controlled by an Agent such that it could be used by that Agent."@en 

- [Resource](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/Resource) [example of usage](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/example_of_usage) "a plot of land"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [Resource](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/Resource) [example of usage](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/example_of_usage) "a group of interns"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [Resource](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/Resource) [elucidation](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/elucidation) "Resources are Resources for some Agent. If no instance of Agent existed, no instance of Resource would exist either. It is not a requirement that something be valuable in order for it to be a Resource. Thus the value of something can drastically change without altering whether that thing is a Resource."@en 

#### Added
- [Resource](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/Resource) [definition](http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#definition) "A Continuant that is owned by, in the possession of, or is otherwise controlled by an Agent such that it could be used by that Agent."@en 

- [Resource](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/Resource) [scopeNote](http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#scopeNote) "Resources are Resources for some Agent. If no instance of Agent existed, no instance of Resource would exist either. It is not a requirement that something be valuable in order for it to be a Resource. Thus the value of something can drastically change without altering whether that thing is a Resource."@en 

- [Resource](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/Resource) [example](http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#example) "a vehicle"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string) 

- [Resource](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/Resource) [example](http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#example) "a knowledge base"^^[string](http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string)

- [Telecommunication Endpoint](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/TelecommunicationEndpoint) [definition](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/definition) "A Telecommunication Network Node that connects a Telecommunication Terminal to a Telecommunication Network."@en 

- [Telecommunication Endpoint](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/TelecommunicationEndpoint) [elucidation](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/elucidation) "A Telecommunication Terminal is an end user device such as a Telephone, fax machine, or Computer."@en 

#### Added
- [Telecommunication Endpoint](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/TelecommunicationEndpoint) [definition](http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#definition) "A Telecommunication Network Node that connects a Telecommunication Terminal to a Telecommunication Network."@en 

- [Telecommunication Endpoint](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/TelecommunicationEndpoint) [scopeNote](http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#scopeNote) "A Telecommunication Terminal is an end user device such as a Telephone, fax machine, or Computer."@en

- [Wired Communication Relay Artifact Function](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/WiredCommunicationRelayArtifactFunction) [definition](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/definition) "A Communication Relay Artifact Function that is realized during events in which an Artifact is used to first receive and then transmit information by means of wires from one Artifact to another for the purpose of communiction."@en

- [Wired Communication Relay Artifact Function](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/WiredCommunicationRelayArtifactFunction) [definition](http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#definition) "A Communication Relay Artifact Function that is realized during events in which an Artifact is used to first receive and then transmit information by means of wires from one Artifact to another for the purpose of communiction."@en 


### Wireless Telecommunication Network `http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/WirelessTelecommunicationNetwork`
#### Removed
- [Wireless Telecommunication Network](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/WirelessTelecommunicationNetwork) [definition](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/definition) "A Telecommunication Network that uses wireless connections to connect Telecommunication Network Nodes."@en 

- [Wireless Telecommunication Network](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/WirelessTelecommunicationNetwork) [alternative label](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/alternative_label) "Wireless Network"@en 

#### Added
- [Wireless Telecommunication Network](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/WirelessTelecommunicationNetwork) [definition](http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#definition) "A Telecommunication Network that uses wireless connections to connect Telecommunication Network Nodes."@en 

- [Wireless Telecommunication Network](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/WirelessTelecommunicationNetwork) [altLabel](http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#altLabel) "Wireless Network"@en 


### X-ray Microscope `http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/XRayMicroscope`
#### Removed
- [X-ray Microscope](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/XRayMicroscope) [definition](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/definition) "A Microscope that is designed to use Electromagnetic Radiation in the soft X-ray band to produce a significantly enlarged image of the Object."@en 

#### Added
- [X-ray Microscope](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/XRayMicroscope) [definition](http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#definition) "A Microscope that is designed to use Electromagnetic Radiation in the soft X-ray band to produce a significantly enlarged image of the Object."@en 


### X-ray Telescope `http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/XRayTelescope`
#### Removed
- [X-ray Telescope](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/XRayTelescope) [definition](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/definition) "A Telescope that is designed to aid in the observation of spatially distant Objects by means of collecting and focusing X-rays to form an enhanced image of the Object."@en 

#### Added
- [X-ray Telescope](http://www.ontologyrepository.com/CommonCoreOntologies/XRayTelescope) [definition](http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#definition) "A Telescope that is designed to aid in the observation of spatially distant Objects by means of collecting and focusing X-rays to form an enhanced image of the Object."@en
